</p>
<ol><li>mourning, funeral

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:траурный.html>тра́урный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráurnyj</b> marš</i> ― <span class="e-translation">funeral/dead march</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:траурный.html>тра́урная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:повязка.html>повя́зка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráurnaja</b> povjázka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crepe band</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mournful, sorrowful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:траурный.html>тра́урный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráurnyj</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation">funereal appearance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трахаться.html>тра́хаться</a> (20759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахать.html>тра́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tráxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахаться.html>тра́хаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tráxatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тра́хнуться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike <i>(against)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mildly vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have sex <i>(with)</i>, to bang, to screw
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потра́хаться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potráxatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тра́хнуться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tráxnutʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be unpleasantly busy with something for a long time

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахея.html>трахе́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">traxéja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахея.html>трахе́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахея.html>трахе́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахея.html>трахе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trachea, windpipe (thin-walled, cartilaginous tube connecting the larynx to the bronchi)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трахнуть.html>тра́хнуть</a> (14856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трах.html>трах</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трахнуть.html>тра́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tráxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bang, to boom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трахнуть.html>тра́хнули</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráxnuli</b> puški</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the guns banged/boomed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crash, to bang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трахнуть.html>тра́хнуть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráxnutʹ</b> kovó-libo po golové</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bang smb on the head</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трахнуть.html>тра́хнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кулак.html>кулако́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tráxnutʹ</b> kulakóm po stolú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bang one's fist on the table; bring one's fist down on the table</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay, to bang, to screw</li></ol>

***треба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́ба</a> (28628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">трѣба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trěba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terba</i>. Displaced the Old East Slavic inherited form <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тереба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tereba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tréba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треба.html>тре́б</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rite, ceremony (an irregular church ceremony performed at the request of a parishioner)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trébovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>demand, request, claim (act of requesting)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовательный.html>тре́бовательный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trébovatelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>exacting, particular, fastidious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:требовательный.html>тре́бовательный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:покупатель.html>покупа́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trébovatelʹnyj</b> pokupátelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hard-to-please customer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>commanding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:требовательный.html>тре́бовательный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:жест.html>жест</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trébovatelʹnyj</b> ton (žest)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">commanding voice (gesture)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***требовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a> (671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">трѣбовати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trěbovati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">трѣбовати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trěbovati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-slavic root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terb-</i> (see <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terba</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trébovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребовать.html>потре́бовать</a></b>) (+ genitive)
</p>
<ol><li>to demand, to request</li>
<li>to need, to call for</li></ol>

</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>  — востребуемый.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-треб-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-у-ем</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требуха.html>требуха́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trebuxá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требуха.html>требухи́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

***тревога.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́га</a> (1602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*trьvoga</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">trwoga</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">тривога</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tryvoha</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвага.html>отва́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvága</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trevóga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alarm, alert</li>
<li>trouble, anxiety, uneasiness, fluster, discomposure, disquiet, disquietude</li></ol>

***тревожить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a> (5392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trevóžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потревожить.html>потрево́жить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревожить.html>встрево́жить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disturb
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Alexander Pushkin,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмах</a> Грузии</cite>  | <cite>On the Hills of Georgia</cite> |  | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://max.mmlc.northwestern.edu/~mdenner/Demo/texts/on_hills_georgia.htm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">"уны́нья <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моего́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жит</a></b>."</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">"Unýnʹja mojevó, ništó ne múčit, ne <b>trevóžit</b>."</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"My melancholy, remains untouched and undisturbed."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to worry, to trouble, to harass</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожиться.html>трево́житься</a> (11715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trevóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожиться.html>трево́житься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trevóžitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">встрево́житься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be anxious/uneasy/worried <i>(about)</i>, to become anxious <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожиться.html>трево́житься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> кого́-либо/что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trevóžitʹsja</b> za kovó-libo/štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worry about someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to trouble oneself, to bother oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрасно.html>напра́сно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожиться.html>трево́жились</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naprásno vy <b>trevóžilisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">you should not have troubled/bothered</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потрево́житься</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrevóžitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trevóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожный.html>трево́жно</a> (4841)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожный.html>трево́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trevóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожный.html>трево́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trevóžno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-трево́жно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)трево́жнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-трево́жно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)трево́жней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>uneasily, alarmedly, with agitation, discomposedly</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>тре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>во́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-тревож-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-н-о</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожный.html>трево́жный</a> (3589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trevóga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alarm, alert, anxiety</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожный.html>трево́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trevóžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)трево́жнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)трево́жней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alarming, disturbing</li>
<li>anxious</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трезвый.html>тре́звый</a> (4323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">трѣзвъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trězvŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terzvъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тверёзый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tverjózyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>

</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трейлер.html>тре́йлер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trɛ́jler</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трейлер.html>тре́йлера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трейлер.html>тре́йлеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трейлер.html>тре́йлеров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trailer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">vehicle towed behind another, used for carrying equipment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
